 The comments 15 agast 2022 ke liye sankalp lenaa he ki ham desh or samaaj kii bhalaai ke liye aage badhenge
 Every department and unit of the government should also get involved in the work
 swabhimani, samrudh, susanskrit, shreshth bharat bananaa he
 By 2022, every citizen has to work to provide electricity to every household
 desh ke anya ganmaanya nagarikon, yuva, sahityakaron or samajaseviyon evam anya ne vishwa bhar main bharat kaa maathaa ooncha karne kaa abhinandaneey kaary kiya
 i heartily wish those countless people from the ramparts of India
 vishwa ke saamne bharat kii vishalata, bharat kii vividhta ke gungan hote rahete hai
 Just as there are many variations of India, there is greatness of India, similarly there is simplicity in the people of India and there is unity in every corner of India
 yahi hamaare desh kii shakti he
 There has been an attempt to refine him in every era
 puraatan paramparaon ke bich yah desh yahaan pahunchaa he
 Our unity, simplicity, brotherhood, harmony are huge capital
 is par kabhi daag nahin laganaa chahie
 If the unity of the country falls apart, the dreams also crumble, that is why the poison of casteism, the passion of the sect is not to be given in any way
 yah desh team india ke kaaran aage bad rahaa he
 This team India is a large team of 125 crore countrymen
 kya duniya ne sochaa he ki sava sau karod deshavaasiyon kii team jab ek hokar lag jaati he, wo raashtra ko badhaati hai or bachaati bhi he
 Where we are trying to reach is due to a team of 125 crore
 loktantr main janabhagidaari sabase badi puunji hoti he
 Team India has only one mandate and that all our arrangements, all the schemes should serve the poor of this country
 ham garibi se mukti kii ladaai ko bal pradaan karnaa chaahate hai
 The poor also want to fight poverty
 15 agast ko aapke saamne kuch vichaar rakhe the, tab main nayaa tha
 What i saw in the beginning was that i had put it in front of the countrymen with no open mind, but today after a year, from the ramparts of the same Red Fort, i assure the countrymen that in a year Team India will get a new With confidence, the new potential deadline has begun to make dreams come true

 bharat jaise desh main agar vikaas kaa pyramid dekhen, to uske sabase neeche kii sataha sabase majboot hoti he

 isliye hamen vikaas ke pyramid ko majboot karnaa he

 " unhone kaha, "trinmul pramukh mamata banerjee ne kuch mudde uthaae hai, jin par sarkaar ke saath vichaar-vimarsh hoga

 Governor, leading to increased corruption in the government
